曾經名噪一時的職業棒球手{{A}}的陰影，在{{B}}的{{C}}中化身為大滿貫投手，統領著這幢龐大且華麗的棒球館。\n哪怕是少女的攀附和球員的臣服，也難以滿足他變質的支配慾。\n他可是球場上擁有最強實力的王者，決不允許任何威脅他地位的存在！={{A}}'s form in the cognitive world. His appearance reflects his distorted desires.
化身為「{{A}}」的惡魔，象徵著{{B}}、散發著扭曲氣息的翅膀，以及充斥著快感的投球機，是他慾望空前膨脹的表現。\n在觀眾如癡如醉的目光中，他投出的必勝絕殺球令隊友瘋狂、令對手肝膽俱裂……\n他就是球場之上唯一的焦點、不朽的傳奇。=Shadow Kiuchi completely distorted by desire. Having lost all sense of self, he can no longer maintain a human form.
一心一意為{{A}}奉獻的啦啦隊少女，身穿明快的制服，洋溢著青春的笑容，眼神中充滿了對{{A}}的狂熱與崇拜。={{A}}'s personal cheerleader born from his cognition. She exists solely to cheer him on.
對{{A}}絕對忠誠的啦啦隊少女，身體輕盈地舞動、活力四射地為{{A}}加油助威，成為賽場之上一道美麗的風景線。={{A}}'s personal cheerleader born from his cognition. She exists solely to cheer him on.

{{A}}本身不會主動攻擊，需要怪盜們在三回合內完成一支<color\=#ff3b37>「神樂之舞」</color>，方可勝利。具體包括如下舞步：\n「癒舞」：使用一次治療技能\n「矛舞」：使用一次攻擊技能\n「劍舞」：使用一次普通攻擊\n「弓舞」：使用一次槍械攻擊\n「物舞」：使用一次道具=<size\=26>{{A}} won't attack, victory when Thieves completed <color\=#ff3b37>[Kagura Dance]</color> within three rounds. 對所有角色造成中量物理屬性傷害，並使所有角色進入『裂傷』狀態，防禦力少量降低，並每回合損失一定生命值，效果持續三回合。=Deal medium Phys damage to all foes, and inflicts all foes with [Laceration], lightly decreases their DEF and makes them lose HP each turn for 3 turns.

倒影=Reflection
受到技能時，驅散一層「倒影」，驅散所有「倒影」時，{{A}}的倒影即死=Dispel 1 stack of [Reflection] when attacked. Die when all [Reflection] are dispelled.
{{A}}的倒影受到攻擊後會驅散一層【倒影】，【倒影】被全部驅散時，{{A}}的倒影即死。=When Reflection of {{A}} is attacked, dispel 1 stack of [Reflection]. Die when all [Reflection] are dispelled.

Gain Final DMG RES and skill usage based on the number of Reflection of {{A}}.</size>"
r:"^1、{{B}}的倒影受到攻擊後會驅散一層【倒影】，每回合恢復三層【倒影】，【倒影】被全部驅散時，{{B}}的倒影即死。\n每存在一個倒影，就會給隊友提供一層【神隱】，受到傷害降低(\d+%)。\n3、每存在一個倒影，給予詭譎的{{B}}和{{A}}額外的技能釋放次數。$"="1. MEMENTOS 4
----------
1、{{A}}會隨機給除自己外的友方角色施加具有保護效果的增益buff。\n2、{{A}}在其回合開始時，會根據場上存在的小怪釋放相應屬性的技能。\n3、小怪死亡一回合後，{{A}}會在其回合結束後重新召喚。=1. {{A}} will randomly gives a protection buff to all other allies. \n2. At the start of {{A}}'s turn, they will use skills based on the minion's element.\n3. After defeating the minion, {{A}} will resummon them at the end of their turn after 1 turn.

r:"^1、進入戰鬥時，召喚天啟四騎士，而後自身進入無敵狀態；天啟四騎士處於<color\=#ff3b37>「生命連結」</color>狀態，當天啟四騎士全部陣亡時，{{F}}陷入狂躁。\n「生命連結」：擁有「生命連結」的單位，受到的傷害按當前生命比例分攤到全部擁有「生命連結」的單位上。\n2、每三個回合，{{F}}及天啟四騎士會各自吹響他們的號角1次，但當其處於精神異常狀態時，無法吹響號角。\n3、{{C}}：得到{{F}}的指示後會在自己的回合開始時吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「瘟疫號角」</color>：隨機使1名怪盜的最終生命值降低；\n4、{{D}}：得到{{F}}的指示後會在自己的回合開始時吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「戰爭號角」</color>：自身獲得持續1回合的<color\=#ff3b37>「戰爭號角」</color>，持續時間內自己受到攻擊時會發起反擊；\n5、{{E}}：得到{{F}}的指示後會在自己的回合開始時吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「饑荒號角」</color>：隨機使1名怪盜釋放技能時的精力消耗提升；\n6、{{B}}：得到{{F}}的指示後會在自己的回合開始時吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「死亡號角」</color>：所有怪盜{{A}}技能的治療效果降低，所有友方獲得2回合的傷害提升；\n7、{{F}}：四位騎士每次吹響號角時會獲得1層<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>；所有騎士都接收到指示後自身會準備一回合，而後吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世號角」</color>：消耗所有<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>對所有怪盜造成萬能傷害（四騎士的攻擊力越高，此次傷害越高），並基於消耗的<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>的層數獲得額外效果。\n1層：最終攻擊力提升(\d+%)；\n2層：傷害提升(\d+%)；\n3層：治療所有騎士(\d+%)的生命值；\n4層：本次傷害必定暴擊。\n8、四騎士首次被全部擊殺後，{{F}}陷入狂躁狀態，立即獻祭自身(\d+%)的生命值復活天啟四騎士，而後自身再次進入無敵狀態；天啟四騎士處於<color\=#ff3b37>「生命連結」</color>狀態，當天啟四騎士全部陣亡時，{{F}}退出無敵狀態。\n「生命連結」：擁有「生命連結」的單位，受到的傷害按當前生命比例分攤到全部擁有「生命連結」的單位上。\n9、狂躁狀態下，自身吹響<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世號角」</color>時，不再消耗<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>，但仍可以根據身上<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>的層數獲得額外效果；每層<color\=#ff3b37>「滅世之力」</color>額外使所有友方獲得一定傷害提升。$"="<size\=24>1. At the start of battle, summons the Four Horsemen, then enters Invincible; The Four Horsemen have <color\=#ff3b37>[Lifelink]</color>, when all Four Horsemen are defeated, {{F}} will enters Manic.\n[Lifelink]: Damage taken by a unit with [Lifelink] is distributed among all [Lifelink] units in proportion to their current HP%.\n2. Every 3 turns, {{F}} and the Four Horsemen will blow their horns, cannot do so when they are inflicted with Mental Ailments.\n3. {{C}}: After receiving orders from {{F}} will use <color\=#ff3b37>[Pestilence Horn]</color>: Randomly decreases 1 Thief's Final HP;\n4. {{D}}: After receiving orders from {{F}} will use <color\=#ff3b37>[War Horn]</color>, will Counter when attacked during the duration; \n5. {{E}}: After receiving orders from {{F}} will use <color\=#ff3b37>[Famine Horn]</color>: Randomly increases 1 Thief's SP cost;\n6. {{B}}: After receiving orders from {{F}} will use <color\=#ff3b37>[Death Horn]</color>: Decreases all Thieves' {{A}} skill Healing Effect and increase all allies' DMG Dealt for 2 turns;\n7. {{F}}: Gains 1 stack of <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color> when the Four Horsemen blow their horns; All Horsemen will use <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Horn]</color> 1 turn after receiving their order: Consumes all <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color> and deals Almighty damage to all Thieves (The higher the Horsemen's ATK, the higher the damage), gains additional effects based on consumed <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color> stacks.\n1 stack: Increases Final ATK by $1;\n2 stacks: Increases DMG Dealt by $2;\n3 stacks: Restores $3 HP to all Horsemen;\n4 stacks: This will Always CRIT.\n8. When you defeat all Four Horsemen, {{F}} will enters Manic, immediately sacrifices $4 HP to revive all Four Horsemen, then enters Invincible; The Four Horsemen have <color\=#ff3b37>[Lifelink]</color>, when all Four Horsemen are defeated, {{F}} will exits Invincible.\n[Lifelink]: Damage taken by a unit with [Lifelink] is distributed among all [Lifelink] units in proportion to their current HP%.\n9. Under Manic, will no longer consumes <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color> when using <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Horn]</color>, but can still gains additional effects from <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color>; Each stack of <color\=#ff3b37>[Apocalypse Power]</color> increases all allies' DMG Dealt.</size>"

瘟疫號角=Pestilence Horn
戰爭號角=War Horn
饑荒號角=Famine Horn
死亡號角=Death Horn
死亡之力=Death Power
滅世號角=Apocalypse Horn
滅世之力=Apocalypse Power
可以用來釋放滅世號角的洪荒之力=Needed for Apocalypse Horn
終末號角=Final Horn

吹號指令=Horn Order
在自己回合開始時，吹響自己的號角=At the start of your turn, blow your horn
吹號準備=Ready Horn
吹號準備中，下個回合開始時吹響自己的號角=Will blow your horn next turn
瘟疫=Pestilence
持續時間內，自身受到攻擊時會發起反擊=Will Counter when attacked during the duration
饑荒=Famine
枯萎=Wither

慾望的女教皇=Priestess of Desire
1、慾望的女教皇進入戰鬥時，會設置戰鬥剩餘時間，戰鬥剩餘時間消耗殆盡時，戰鬥失敗。\n2、慾望的女教皇每次釋放「失控的邀請」時，會大幅減少戰鬥剩餘時間；與此同時，慾望的女教皇會召喚一波隨從並使自己處於「無法被選中」的狀態，當所有隨從被擊殺或逃跑後，慾望的女教皇會從「無法被選中」的狀態中退出。\n3、隨從逃跑後，慾望的女教皇每個回合都會釋放「教義的懲罰」，逃跑的隨從越多，造成的傷害就越高。=1. At the start of battle, Priestess of Desire sets a timer, you lose if the timer reaches zero.\n2. When Priestess of Desire uses [Invitation to Chaos], heavily decrease remaining time; then summons a wave of minions and becomes [Untargetable], exits [Untargetable] when all minions are defeated or escaped. \n3. After minions escaped, Priestess of Desire will use [Doctrine Punishment] each turn, the more escaped minions, the higher the damage.
1、慾望的女教皇進入戰鬥時，會設置戰鬥剩餘時間，戰鬥剩餘時間消耗殆盡時，戰鬥失敗。\n2、慾望的女教皇每次釋放「失控的邀請」時，會大幅減少戰鬥剩餘時間；與此同時，慾望的女教皇會召喚一波隨從並使自己處於「無法被選中」的狀態，當所有隨從被擊殺或逃跑後，慾望的女教皇會從「無法被選中」的狀態中退出。\n3、隨從被擊殺時，會增加戰鬥剩餘時間；但是隨從會在一定回合後逃跑。\n4、隨從逃跑後，慾望的女教皇每個回合都會釋放「教義的懲罰」，逃跑的隨從越多，造成的傷害就越高。=1. At the start of battle, Priestess of Desire sets a timer, you lose if the timer reaches zero.\n2. When Priestess of Desire uses [Invitation to Chaos], heavily decrease remaining time; then summons a wave of minions and becomes [Untargetable], exits [Untargetable] when all minions are defeated or escaped. \n3. When minions are defeated, extends the timer; but they will escape after a set number of turns.\n4. After minions escaped, Priestess of Desire will use [Doctrine Punishment] each turn, the more escaped minions, the higher the damage.
